# List of supported chips

*For an explanation of the requirements tab, please have a look at [REQUIREMENTS](./REQUIREMENTS.md) document.*

## CONTENT

- [List of supported chips](#list-of-supported-chips)
  - [CONTENT](#content)
    - [DSPIC](#dspic)
    - [AVR](#avr)
    - [GIGADEVICE](#gigadevice)
    - [TIVA](#tiva)
    - [NXP](#nxp)
    - [PIC32](#pic32)
    - [PIC18](#pic18)
    - [STM32](#stm32)

> ***NOTE:***
>> <a name="note_1">:one:</a> Chip doesn't have the minimum required amount of SRAM,
>> but has been added regardless as it is the default chip
>> for EasyPIC v7 system.
